<Review>I've just finished re-furnishing our house with Scandinavian Designs furniture (our old furniture went to our son's house in Tahoe). We have been customers of Scandinavian Designs for more than 20 years.
This current shopping process lasted about a month and included several visits to the store as well as several emails and telephone calls.
From the start we dealt with Irina Alexander (and the store manager Turi).
Irina was personable, knowledgeable and attentive--a true professional.  Nothing was too much trouble.  Our overall showroom experience with Scandinavian Designs, and Irina in particular, was first class.
We had two large orders--one delivered in the East Bay and the other delivered to Tahoe.  The firms Scandinavian Designs used for delivery were also extremely good--on time, with good communications about arrival windows.

< Review>
We had a really pleasant shopping experience during the Black Friday Sales event. Gary, the sales person was very patient and helpful. He allowed us to roam around the whole store and explore, while answering all of our questions in regards color schemes and pairings available. This is probably one of very few furniture/home furnishing stores where sales reps do not hover over your head and try to persuade you to make a purchase immediately. Needless to say, the furniture at Scandinavian Designs sells itself and once you try out some of the pieces you will want to own all of them. We selected a couple of electronically reclining couches for our new living room, as well as a media center, a full set of side tables, a rug and two giant oil paintings to tie it all together, as well as a dining table and 6 chair set. They should be delivered this week and we will update the review once delivery takes place and we have a chance to use and enjoy our new furniture. It's rare to find things on sale at Scandinavian Designs and we wanted to capitalize on the opportunity to own some really nice high end pieces. We will come back when we need to remodel the bedrooms as there were some very modern and appealing sets available, but our budget was already maxed out.</Review>

< review>
Juice Crafters is a very solid juicer/smoothie bar although a bit expensive for the average consumer.  Drinks range usually well above $5 for the most part along with some food items like acai bowls.  They have things like ginger shots to healthy smoothies that are mindful of your body and energy for the day.

I usually like to get the muscle builder (a delicious protein smoothie) as my go to drink which costs about $8 to begin with.  They also have a stamp card which you can fill out to get a free drink after a certain amount of purchases.

Parking-wise, like everything in this area of Brentwood, there is limited street parking which will be tough to find during the daytime.  You may want to opt to park a bit further and walk to this area instead.< /review>

<Text>Muji Santa Anita opened on January 12th, 2017. Muji makes unbranded high-quality stationary, home goods and other accessories.

Muji is a Japanese minimalistic-design centric store. The price point is higher l, but the quality and design is outstanding.

The layout of the store is fairly straightforward. As you walk in, stationary (Notebook and pens) and their humidifiers are in the first section. On the left side, there are some clothing. From there on, there are home accessories Suh as clocks and plates. Further inside are the cookware and cleaning accessories used in home.

Muji Santa Anita has a unique stamp station in which consumers can use cute stamps to personalize the notebooks they buy. (See Picture)

If you love minimalism and quality, this store is definitely worth a visit.</Text>< time>

< review>
They sell home goods, stationary, and clothes that are too small to fit a lot of people.

Their gimick is that they don't brand anything. Everything is in plain packaging and the designs are all very minimalist. The upside is that everything looks very modern and they fit in well with whatever decor you have. Quality is pretty high, and while I would say most of their products are a bit overpriced, they are worth the price. Most of their notebooks are very good for writing with fountain pens, which is great because they also sell a fountain pen.</review>

<review>I rarely post reviews for products online as I'm seldom impressed with a product enough to do so.  However, in this instance I feel compelled to shout this one from the rooftops!  I am the full time caregiver for my 64 spouse who I've been married to for 46 years.  She has Type II diabetes among other serious maladies, but her blood sugar drops dangerously low without warning, often in her sleep.  With the new Libre II device monitoring her levels in real time and sounding the alarm, we are able to promptly react before she goes into hypoglycemic shock.  Just as amazing is the predictive nature of the device that forecasts rising or falling trends of her lab values thus allowing us to adjust diet and other factors resulting using less insulin.  It is a game changer for us!  Finally, we are so grateful to Advanced Diabetes Supply for guiding us through the process of obtaining the device, coordinating medical records, insurance company requirements and keeping us posted every step of the way! **FINAL UPDATE**
At first, I was very unhappy with ADS customer service for the reasons below. However, ADS was extremely proactive in remedying the situation and now I am extremely satisfied. As soon as my insurance approved the authorization, ADS got my order ready and out the door. I believe that my initial experience was not representative of ADS as a whole and I applaud their customer service department for going above and beyond to make sure I could get my supplies as fast as possible.

**UPDATE**
So, I'm actually really impressed with ADS customer service! Less than one day after I posted the original review, a rep contacted me and helped me get everything sorted out. It turns out we do need some more paperwork (which I found a little frustrating, because I was told multiple times by multiple reps that they had all the paperwork necessary and all I had to do was wait), but hopefully that was the last of the miscommunication. They also apologized for the lack of communication on behalf of the company and even offered to overnight me some testing materials so that I can check my blood sugars in the meantime. This interaction makes me hopeful that my previous experience with ADS was not representative of their customer service. I don't like leaving bad reviews on yelp, but I think that a company that deals with life-saving medical supplies should be held to a higher standard than say, a coffee shop. I will update this review hopefully just one more time after everything works out and I actually get my G6 system!

I've been trying to get on the Dexcom G6 and my experience with Advanced Diabetes Supply has extremely been frustrating. The process of getting the supplies I need has been delayed multiple times because different reps keep giving me the wrong information. They even sent a text message that an authorization had been submitted, but when I called to check in, it actually had not been submitted. To their credit, every rep I spoke to has been very friendly. My experience is detailed below:

ADS: "We spoke with your doctor's office yesterday, we have all the paperwork, and everything looks good. We'll give you a call when things are ready."

Me: *calls to check in two weeks later*

ADS: "Actually, we need your doctor's office to send us a form so we can send it to your insurance. After we get that, it'll take about a week for your insurance to approve it."

Me: ??? then why did you tell me everything was good and have me wait two weeks for nothing??? *Has doctor submit necessary paperwork in less than one day. calls ADS to check in a week later."

ADS: "Yes, we have all the paperwork and we just have to submit an authorization to your insurance. I'll submit it now, check back in a few days."

**They actually sent me a text message which states that the authorization was submitted as urgent and everything should be approved in about a week.

Me: *calls back a few days later to check AGAIN*

ADS: "Your authorization hasn't been submitted.... Yes, I see that someone sent you that text message, but they didn't actually submit the authorization. I'll submit it now and everything should be ready in about a week."

Me: ??????? Your company literally sent me a text message that my authorization had been submitted as "URGENT" and that I would only have to wait another week. Now my process of waiting a week is starting over??

Extremely frustrating... will be calling back tomorrow to see if they actually submitted the authorization.< /Review>

<Time>1450421172945<//Time><Rate>5<//Rate><text>Very highly recommended. This location is "new" - that is, although the buildings have been here for some time, the property has only just recently become part of the Extra Space brand...and they've done a thorough facelift on the place. I've been to a number of self storage places over the years, including some other ExtraSpace locations, and they always feel vaguely horror-movie-ish...long,  scary hallways with flickering light bulbs, rusty elevators and creaky doors. Not so at this place. SUPER clean, well-lit hallways inside AND plenty of floodlights outside, and freshly painted. Units are odor free, individually alarmed, and well lit  also.

My only suggestion is adding doorstops at the hallway entrances, and smoothing out the transitions from the ground outside to the concrete floor of the hallways...as it is, the slight lip of the concrete sometimes makes it difficult to roll a hand truck through the door.

Keep it up!<//text>< Pictures>
